    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">With an eye towards future-proofing AI systems, Unit 42 researchers contribute to a growing body of knowledge that helps anticipate and mitigate potential security threats surrounding LLMs. 

This article discusses a new jailbreak technique named "Deceptive Delight," which disguises harmful content within benign contexts. The findings underlines the nuanced nature of AI model vulnerabilities. To counteract these manipulations, we urge implementing strong content filters and carefully limiting prompt engineering. <a class="link" href="https://bit.ly/3A8gDEL?trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://bit.ly/3A8gDEL</a></p>

Details at <a class="link" href="https://bit.ly/48aTOgd?trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://bit.ly/48aTOgd</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Beware of fake shopping <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fscam&amp;trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#scam</a> sites! We identified a recent campaign using malicious infra to set up bogus online stores titled "Penguin Mall" including a <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdropcaught&amp;trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#dropcaught</a> domain. These sites only accept cryptocurrency for payment. More info at <a class="link" href="https://bit.ly/4dKqtuh?trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://bit.ly/4dKqtuh</a>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Recent findings reveal that Lynx <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fransomware&amp;trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ransomware</a>, a rebrand of INC ransomware, is targeting industries such as retail and financial services in the US and UK, among other sectors. This article summarizes the current movements of this <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fraas&amp;trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#RaaS</a> to pinpoint how security analysts can strengthen their defenses against any attack vectors. <a class="link" href="https://bit.ly/3zIvEgx?trk=public_post_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="public_post_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://bit.ly/3zIvEgx</a></p>
